var cls=act==='COMPRAR'?'buy':act==='VENDER'?'sell':'wait'; gid('sigArea').className='sig-area '+cls; gid('sigTag').textContent=act==='COMPRAR'?'SEÑAL LARGA':act==='VENDER'?'SEÑAL CORTA':'SIN OPERACIÓN'; gid('sigAction').textContent=act==='COMPRAR'?'↑ COMPRAR':act==='VENDER'?'↓ VENDER':'◆ ESPERAR'; gid('sigEntry').textContent=d.entrada||'—'; gid('sigExit').textContent=d.salida||'—'; gid('sigStop').textContent=d.stop_loss||'—'; gid('sigTime').textContent=d.tiempo_estimado?'⏱ '+d.tiempo_estimado:''; gid('sigReason').innerHTML=(d.razon||'').replace(/\*\*(.*?)\*\*/g,'$1'); var conf=Math.min(100,Math.max(0,d.confianza||50)); gid('confPct').textContent=conf+'%'; if(act!=='ESPERAR'){ var isBuy=act==='COMPRAR'; var entryPrice=isBuy?Math.round((p+SPREAD/2)*1000)/1000:Math.round((p-SPREAD/2)*1000)/1000; var mins=60; if(d.tiempo_estimado){var m=d.tiempo_estimado.match(/\d+/);if(m)mins=Math.min(90,Math.max(10,parseInt(m[0])));} S.log.push({ id:Date.now(),time:fmtT(),accion:act,entryPrice:entryPrice, targetPrice:d.salida?parseFloat(d.salida.replace('$','')):null, stopPrice:d.stop_loss?parseFloat(d.stop_loss.replace('$','')):null, checkAt:Date.now()+mins*60*1000,result:null,closePrice:null }); sv();renderLog();updateTracker();drawChart(); }else{ gid('tracker').className='tracker'; } } function checkPendingLog(){ if(!S.lp)return;var changed=false; S.log.forEach(function(e){ if(e.result!==null)return; var isBuy=e.accion==='COMPRAR',cp=S.lp,move=isBuy?cp-e.entryPrice:e.entryPrice-cp; var resolved=false; if(e.targetPrice&&(isBuy?cp>=e.targetPrice:cp<=e.targetPrice)){e.result='win';e.closeReason='target';e.closePrice=cp;resolved=true;} if(!resolved&&e.stopPrice&&(isBuy?cp<=e.stopPrice:cp>=e.stopPrice)){e.result='loss';e.closeReason='stop';e.closePrice=cp;resolved=true;} if(!resolved&&Date.now()>=e.checkAt){var win=move>0;e.result=win?'win':'loss';e.closeReason=win?'timeout_win':'timeout_loss';e.closePrice=cp;resolved=true;} if(resolved){changed=true;} }); if(changed){sv();renderLog();updateTracker();drawChart();} } function renderLog(){ var wins=S.log.filter(function(e){return e.result==='win';}).length; var total=S.log.filter(function(e){return e.result!==null;}).length;
